)@@G@@CLJD))@C@@@@^@)^@)^@)^@)^@) S$C1JEK$^@)^@) 0)C1J*[@@@@*SDFF*@G@@@@      HV
)@@G@@    . THIS ROUTINE HANDLES ALL FORMS OF LOCATE, FIND AND CHANGE   @^@@@@HW
)@@G@@          . COMMANDS.   @^@@@@          AXR$      .   @^@@@@          EDHX
)@@G@@PC      .   @^@@@@$(1)      . I BANK CODE.@^@@@@          LIT     .     HY
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ASCII   . SET ASCII.@G@@@@.         THIS SECTION OF CODEHZ
)@@G@@ HANDLES VARIOUS FORMS OF 'FIND' COMMANDS.@[@@@@.     @E@@@@SNOOP     EQIA
)@@G@@U       0                 . SET SNOOPY FLAG.    @D@@@@OLDC      EQU     IB
)@@G@@  1                 . TURN ON OLD.  @G@@@@          . THE ENTRIES BELOW IC
)@@G@@ARE OLD COMMANDS WHICH WILL BE DROPPED    @^@@@@          . SOMEDAY..   ID
)@@G@@@E@@@@          ON        OLDC              . ASM IF OLD REQUIRED.@#@@@@IE
)@@G@@FP1*      . FP    @B@@@@          LMJ       X9,LFMOD          .   @C@@@@IF
)@@G@@          S         X9,PTFLG          . SET.    @E@@@@          J       IG
)@@G@@  FIND11            . ENTER BELOW MOD GET.@#@@@@FCD1*     . FCD.  @B@@@@IH
)@@G@@          LMJ       X9,LFMOD          .   @B@@@@          S         X9,FII
)@@G@@LDFLG         .   @D@@@@          J         FC11              . SET FC TIJ
)@@G@@OO.   @#@@@@FD1*      . FD.   @B@@@@          LMJ       X9,LFMOD        IK
)@@G@@  .   @B@@@@          S         X9,FLDFLG         .   @B@@@@          J IL
)@@G@@K     @H@@@9         SLBD  A9,18         . SHIFT POINTERS TO UPPER HALVEIM
)@@G@@S OF REGISTERS    @F@@@9IGMOV7   LABEL . MERGE TO CONTINUE SEARCH FOR ININ
)@@G@@TERNAL POINTERS   @E@@@9         MSW   A9,0,*A2      . SEARCH FOR INTERNIO
)@@G@@AL POINTERS @C@@@9         GOTO  IGMOV6        . -> SEARCH IS DONE@F@@@9IP
)@@G@@         ANU,U A2,1          . BACK INDEX UP TO WORD JUST LOCATED @C@@@9IQ
)@@G@@         LOAD  X5,W1H1,A3    . LOAD THE POINTER @E@@@9         ADD   X5,IR
)@@G@@X4         . ADD IN THE APPROPRIATE OFFSET@ @@@9         STORE X5,W1H1,AIS
)@@G@@3    .@D@@@9         GOTO  IGMOV7        . -> CONTINUE SEARCH     @B@@@9IT
)@@G@@IGMOV6   LABEL . TRANSFER THE STACK ITEMS @C@@@9         LOAD  R1,A8    IU
)@@G@@     . RESET BT COUNTER @B@@@9         BT    X3,0,*X2      . MOVE ITEMS IV
)@@G@@@D@@@9         GOTO  GEND0         . -> CHECK FOR COMPLETION@B@@@9IGMVI0IW
)@@G@@    LABEL .            OR IGXI0     @C@@@9          LINK   GARGMK .     IX
)@@G@@          GET MASK@D@@@9         JP    A9,IGMVI1     .                **IY
)@@G@@***** @ @@@9         LXOR  A7,DGFLGZ     .@ @@@9IGMVI1   LABEL          IZ
)@@G@@     .@E@@@9          STORE  A7,DGFLGZ .            SET GLOBAL FLAGS    JA
)@@G@@@C@@@9         GOTO  GEND0 .             -> NEXT ICODE@#@@@9IGOI0     LAJB
)@@G@@BEL . @C@@@9          LINK   GARGMK .               GET MASK@G@@@9      JC
)@@G@@   JN    A9,IGNI0      . -> REALLY FLAG AND DGFLGZ         *******@E@@@9JD
)@@G@@          LOR    A7,DGFLGZ .            SET SELECTED FLAGS  @ @@@9      JE
)@@G@@    STORE  A7,DGFLGZ .  @^@@@9         GOTO  GEND0 .  @#@@@9IGNI0     LAJF
)@@G@@BEL . @ @@@9          LAND   A7,DGFLGZ .  @G@@@9          STORE  A7,DGFLJG
)@@G@@GZ .            -> PROCESS NEXT INSTRUCTION     @^@@@9         GOTO  GENJH
)@@G@@D0 .  @C@@@9IGBRC0   LABEL .                   GENERATE JUMP@B@@@9      JI
)@@G@@   LINK  GARG .              GET AW @ @@@9         USING  AWDS,X2 .     JJ
)@@G@@@D@@@9         LOAD  A7,0742000,I .      GET JUMP OP CODE   @^@@@9      JK
)@@G@@   SLB   A7,18 .  @F@@@9IGBRC3   LABEL               . MERGE POINT FROM JL
)@@G@@CONDITIONAL JUMP  @G@@@9         ADD   A7,AWOFST .         ADD IN U FILEJM
)@@G@@D OR ELSE NEXT INST     @E@@@9         IF    AWRGPT,ZERO THEN,IGBRC1 . -JN
)@@G@@> NO ADDRESS YET  @#@@@9IGBRC2   LABEL .  @D@@@9         STORE A7,CDINSTJO
)@@G@@,*X10 .     SET JUMP INST     @C@@@9         GCORE 0 'LABEL',GEND0 . RESJP
)@@G@@ERVE SPACE  @#@@@9IGBRC1   LABEL .  @D@@@9         STORE X10,AWOFST .   JQ
)@@G@@     SET PTR TO INST    @^@@@9         GOTO  IGBRC2 . @#@@@9IGLABEL   LAJR
)@@G@@BEL . @F@@@9          LINK   GARG .                 GET REFERENCE TO LABJS
)@@G@@EL    @C@@@9         LOAD  X3,X2 .             SAVE AW PTR  @#@@@9IGLABEJT
)@@G@@L1  LABEL . @^@@@9         USING WORD,X2 .@D@@@9         LOAD  A7,W1H2 .JU
)@@G@@           GET UFIELD OF INST @F@@@9         STORE X10,W1H2,X2 .       SJV
)@@G@@ET U FIELD IN BRANCH INST     @F@@@9         IF    A7,EQ,0,I THEN,IGLBL2JW
)@@G@@ . -> END OF CHAIN, SET PTR   @^@@@9         LOAD  X2,A7 .  @E@@@9      JX
)@@G@@    GOTO   IGLABEL1 .             TEST NEXT REFERENCE @#@@@9IGLBL2   LABJY
)@@G@@EL .  @D@@@9         STORE X10,W1,X3 .         SET AW PTR TO CODE @C@@@9JZ
)@@G@@         GOTO  GEND0 .             -> NEXT ICODE@ @@@9          USING  WKA
)@@G@@ORD,X5 .    @#@@@9IGBAL0    LABEL . @C@@@9         LINK  GADRAW .       KB
)@@G@@     GET ADDRESS  @D@@@9         STORE X1,DGLKSK .         SAVE ICDOE PTKC
)@@G@@R     @ @@@9         STORE A1,DGLKS2 .    @D@@@9         SET   DGXTDL,ONKD
)@@G@@     . SET SUBROUTINE FLAG    @C@@@9         GOTO  IGGOTO1 .           -KE
)@@G@@> BRANCH    @#@@@9IGGOTO0   LABEL . @C@@@9         LINK  GADRAW .       KF
)@@G@@     GET ADDRESS  @#@@@9IGGOTO1  LABEL .  @^@'@9         SETGC 6,0,X5 . KG
)@@G@@@^@@@'.        SETGC 6,0,X5 . @ @@@'         LOADXM  X1,W1U,X5 .  @ @@@'KH
)@@G@@         LOAD    A1,KLCH6W .  @F@@@9          GOTO   GNEXT .            KI
)@@G@@    -> PROCESS NEW IGEN INST  @#@@@9IGAPPN0   LABEL . @C@@@9         LINKJ
)@@G@@K  GADRAW .            GET ADDESS   @G@@@9         LMJ   X11,0,X5 .     KK
)@@G@@     GO TO ROUTINE                 *******@G@@@9          GOTO   GEND0 .KL
)@@G@@                -> RETURN PROCESS INST AT (X5)  @#@@@9IGON0     LABEL . KM
)@@G@@@C@@@9         GETC .                    GET FLAGS    @E@@@9         SLBKN
)@@G@@D  A7,6+36 .           GET FULL 9 (12) BIT FLAG @#@@@9         GETC .   KO
)@@G@@@D@@@9         ADD   A7,A8 .       ADD IN LOWER PART OF FLAG@C@@@9      KP
)@@G@@   AND,H2 A7,DGFLGZ-(IN 63,H2,1,0)  .     @E@@@9         JP    A9,IGOFF0KQ
)@@G@@ .   -> CHECKING OFF INSTEAD OF ON  @D@@@9         JNZ   A8,IGGOTO0 .   KR
)@@G@@     -> SOME BITS ON .  @C@@@9         GOTO  GEND1 .             IGNORE KS
)@@G@@ICODE @#@@@9IGOFF0    LABEL . @C@@@9         JZ    A8,IGGOTO0 .        -KT
)@@G@@> ALL OFF . @^@@@9         GOTO  GEND1    @#@@@9IGRTRN0   LABEL . @D@@@9KU
)@@G@@         LOADXM X1,DGLKSK .        RESET ICODE STACK  @ @@@9         LOAKV
)@@G@@DXM A1,DGLKS2 .   @E@@@9         SET   DGXTDL,OFF    . TURN OFF SUBROUTIKW
)@@G@@NE FLAG     @C@@@9         GOTO  GEND0 .             -> NEXT ICODE@#@@@9KX
)@@G@@IGSET0    LABEL . @^@@@9          LINK   GARG . @E@@@9          LOAD   XKY
)@@G@@3,X2 .                X3 -> LEFT OPERAND  @E@@@9          LINK   GARG . KZ
)@@G@@                X2 -> RIGHT OPERAND @C@@@9         LOAD  A2,0,X2 .      LA
)@@G@@     A2=AW MOVED  @^@@@9         STORE A2,0,X3 .@F@@@9         AND   A2,LB
)@@G@@RGMSK2 .   GET RID OF KEEP BIT AND RGSW POINTER @C@@@9         IF    A3,LC
)@@G@@NE,0,I THEN,GEND0 . -> NOT RAW@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,A2 .    @E@@@9LD
)@@G@@         SUB   X2,RGSWUR . CHECK IF RSW POINTS BACK TO RAW  @F@@@9      LE
)@@G@@   IF    X2,NZERO THEN,GEND0 . -> RGSW DID NOT POINT TO AW  @E@@@9      LF
)@@G@@    STORE  X3,RGSWUR .            UPDATE RGSW POINTER @C@@@9         GOTLG
)@@G@@O  GEND0 .             -> NEXT ICODE@#@@@9IGLOAD0  LABEL .  @G@@@9      LH
)@@G@@   LINK  GARG .        GET AW <- X2 AND NUMBER OF WORDS IN A10    @D@@@9LI
)@@G@@         IF    A10,NE,2,I THEN,GLOADB . -> FIXED LOAD @C@@@9         LINLJ
)@@G@@K  RGGETFPR .          GET 2 WORDS  @D@@@9         LOAD  A7,071,I .     LK
)@@G@@     SET FLOAT LOAD     @D@@@9         LOAD  A10,013,I .         SET FLOLL
)@@G@@AT J FIELD  @C@@@9         GOTO  GLOAD1 .            -> MERGE     @#@@@9LM
)@@G@@GLOADB   LABEL .  @G@@@9         IF    A10,NE,3,I THEN,GLOADC . -> ONE WLN
)@@G@@ORD 'A' REGISTER LOAD   @C@@@9         LINK  RGGETXRG .    GET X REGISTELO
)@@G@@R     @C@@@9         LOAD  A7,027,I . LOAD OPCODE FOR LOAD X@D@@@9      LP
)@@G@@   GOTO  GLOAD2 . -> MERGE WITH ONE WORD LOAD   @C@@@9GLOADC   LABEL . LLQ
)@@G@@OAD ONE WORD 'A' REGISTER     @D@@@9          LINK   RGGETGPR .         LR
)@@G@@    ->GET REGISTER@D@@@9         LOAD  A7,010,I .          SET FIXED LOALS
)@@G@@D     @C@@@9GLOAD2   LABEL . MERGE POINT FOR ALL WORD LOADS @C@@@9      LT
)@@G@@   LOAD  A10,0,I .           SET J FIELD  @#@@@9GLOAD1    LABEL . @C@@@9LU
)@@G@@         STORE A7,DGOPCD .         SET OP CODE  @C@@@9         STORE A10LV
)@@G@@,DGJCOD .        SAVE J FIELD @C@@@9         LOAD  X3,X5 .             GLW
)@@G@@ET ARGUMENT @F@@@9         LOAD  X5,X2 .             SET PARAMETER TO FRLX
)@@G@@EE ROUTINE  @G@@@9          LINK   GFREE0 .               ->FREE OPERANDLY
)@@G@@ IF NECESSARY     @C@@@9         LOAD  A10,DGJCOD .        SAVE J FIELD LZ
)@@G@@@F@@@9          LINK   IGRXLD .               ->GENERATE RX FORM OF LOADMA
)@@G@@@ @@@9          USING  RGSWRD,X3 .  @F@@@9          STORE  X2,RGSWUR .  MB
)@@G@@          LINK NEW USER TO REGISTER @ @@@9          STORE  X3,0,X2 .    MC
)@@G@@@C@@@9         GOTO  GEND0 .             -> NEXT ICODE@#@@@9IGSHIFT  LABMD
)@@G@@EL .  @D@@@9          LINK   RGXLD .                 GET OPERAND  @F@@@9ME
)@@G@@         LOAD  X5,0,X2 .           X5=A(RGSW) OF REG TO BE SHIFTED@ @@@9MF
)@@G@@         USING RGSWRD,X5 .    @G@@@9         LOAD  A7,010001,I   . PREPAMG
)@@G@@RE TO ADD 1 TO REG NUM AND ADDRESS  @D@@@9         LOAD  A6,RGSWRN .    MH
)@@G@@     GET REG NUMBER     @A@@@9         IF    A6,ODD THEN,IGSH2 .  @F@@@9MI
)@@G@@         LOADN A7,010001,I   . SUBTRACT 1 FROM REG NUM AND ADDRESS@E@@@9MJ
)@@G@@IGSH2    LABEL     . SHIFT REGISTER NUMBERS IN EVEN-ODD PAIR@E@@@9      MK
)@@G@@   ADD   A7,RGSWIF .   ADD IN REGISTER NUM AND ADDRESS@G@@@9         IF ML
)@@G@@   A6,NE,A15-A0,I THEN,IGSH3 . -> NOT A15-A16, SET SHIFT    @C@@@9      MM
)@@G@@   LOAD  A10,X2        . SAVE AW POINTER  @D@@@9         LOADA X2,DRSW15MN
)@@G@@ .   POINT TO RSW OF A15 - A16@G@@@9         LOAD  A3,RGSWUF     . GET PMO
)@@G@@OINTER TO FROUNT OF IN-USE LIST     @H@@@9         IF    A3,NE,X2 THEN,IMP
)@@G@@GSH4 . -> A15 IS NOT FIRST AVAILABLE USED REG   @D@@@9         LOADA A3,MQ
)@@G@@RGSWFF     . POINT TO FREE LIST HEAD@G@@@9         IF    A3,NE,RGSWFB THMR
)@@G@@EN,IGSH4 . -> THERE EXISTS A FREE REGISTER@H@@@9         LINK  RGUNLINK MS
)@@G@@     . REMOVE RSW(A15-A16) FROM FROUNT OF IN-USE LIST @H@@@9         LOAMT
)@@G@@D  X3,RGSWUB     . X3 -> CELL AFTER WHICH RSW(A15) TO BE ADDED    @F@@@9MU
)@@G@@         LINK  RGLINK        . PUT RSW(A15) AT BACK OF IN-USE LIST@G@@@9MV
)@@G@@IGSH4    LABEL . MERGE POINT WHEN A15 WILL NOT BE USED TO LOAD ITSELF   MW
)@@G@@@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X2     .@G@@@9         IF    RGSW1W,ON,RGSWKMX
)@@G@@Y THEN,IGSH5 . -> 1 WORD REGISTER TYPE    @D@@@9         LINK  RGGETFPR MY
)@@G@@     . GET 2-WORD REGISTER    @ @@@9         GOTO  IGSH6         .@ @@@9MZ
)@@G@@IGSH5    LABEL               .@D@@@9         LINK  RGGETGPR      . GET 1NA
)@@G@@-WORD REGISTER    @G@@@9IGSH6    LABEL               . MERGE HERE AFTER NB
)@@G@@NEW RESISTER OBTAINED   @F@@@9         LOAD  A7,RGOP4      . GET CIRCULANC
)@@G@@RILY SHIFTED DL A0,A15  @ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5     .@F@@@9      ND
)@@G@@   ADD   A7,RGSWRN     . ADD TO A0 THE OFFSET OF REG PAIR   @I@@@9      NE
)@@G@@   LSSC  A7,22         . SHIFT DL A0+OFFSET,A15 INTO PROPER FORMAT *****NF
)@@G@@**    @D@@@9         STORE A7,CDINST,*X10 .    SET INSTRUCTION    @C@@@9NG
)@@G@@         GCORE 0 .                 RESERVE SPACE@D@@@9         LOAD  X2,NH
)@@G@@A10        . GET SAVED POINTER TO AW@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5     .NI
)@@G@@@D@@@9         STORE X2,RGSWUR     . POINT RSW(NEW) TO AW   @F@@@9      NJ

)@@G@@ AFTER WHICH NEW CELL IS TO BE ADDED@#@@@9RGLINK   LLOC .   @ @@@9      WE
)@@G@@   LOAD  X4,W1H1,X3 .   @ @@@9         STORE X4,W1H1,X2 .   @F@@@9      WF
)@@G@@   STORE X3,W1H2,X2 .        SET FLNK AND BLNK OF NEW CELL  @F@@@9      WG
)@@G@@   STORE X2,W1H2,X4 .        SET BLNK OF FOLLOWING CELL     @E@@@9      WH
)@@G@@   STORE X2,W1H1,X3 .        SET FLNK OF PREC CELL    @C@@@9         LJMWI
)@@G@@P .                    -> RETURN    @^@@@9. CALL   LINK  RGFREE   @C@@@9WJ
)@@G@@.        X5=A(RGSW) OF REGISTER TO BE FREED     @#@@@9. RETURN NONE     WK
)@@G@@@G@@@9. ACTION REMOVES REGISTER FROM IN-USE LIST AND RETURNS IT TO FREE WL
)@@G@@LIST  @#@@@9. DESTROY NONE    @#@@@9RGFREE    LOCAL . @ @@@9         STOWM
)@@G@@RE X2,DRGSAV .    @ @@@9         STORE X3,DRGSAV+1 .  @ @@@9         STOWN
)@@G@@RE X4,DRGSAV+2 .  @C@@@9         STORE A7,DRGSAV+3 .       SAVE A7 ALSO WO
)@@G@@@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5 .    @ @@@9         LOAD  A7,RGSWBL .    WP
)@@G@@@F@@@9         IF    A7,GE,0177777,I THEN,RGXR . -> NOT MANAGED, RETURN WQ
)@@G@@@E@@@9         LOADA A7,RGSXFB .         PREPARE TO ADD X REG     @C@@@9WR
)@@G@@         LOAD  A3,RGSWKY .         SEE IF X REG @D@@@9         IF    A3,WS
)@@G@@GE,RGSWXR,I THEN,RGFROK . -> OK FREE@C@@@9         LOADA A7,RGSWFB .    WT
)@@G@@     ADD A REG    @E@@@9         LINK  RGODD .             RESET ACC TO WU
)@@G@@ODD REG     @#@@@9RGFROK   LABEL .  @D@@@9          USING WORD,X2 .     WV
)@@G@@          SET WORD DSECT@E@@@9         AND,U A3,RGSWXR .   CLEAR FLAGS EWW
)@@G@@XCEPT X-REG FLAG  @G@@@9         STORE  A4,RGSWKY .        RESET FLAGS  WX
)@@G@@                 *******@E@@@9         LOAD  X2,X5 .             POINT TWY
)@@G@@O RGSW TO UNLINK  @E@@@9         LINK  RGUNLINK .          UNLINK FROM UWZ
)@@G@@SED LIST    @E@@@9          LOAD   X3,A7 .                ADD TO NEW LISXA
)@@G@@T     @G@@@9          LINK   RGLINK .               PUT REG AT END OF FRXB
)@@G@@EE LIST     @B@@@9         GOTO  RGXR .              RETURN @ @@@9      XC
)@@G@@   USING RGSWRD,X5     .@#@@@9RGODD    LLOC .   @E@@@9         LOAD  A6,XD
)@@G@@RGSWIF .         GET REG NUMBER AND ADDR  @D@@@9         IF    A6,ODD THXE
)@@G@@EN,LJMP .   -> ALREADY SET    @F@@@9         SUB   A6,010001,I   . SUBTRXF
)@@G@@ACT TO MAKE ADDR AND NUM ODD  @ @@@9         STORE A6,RGSWIF .    @C@@@9XG
)@@G@@         LJMP .                    -> RETURN    @ @@@9          USING  WXH
)@@G@@ORD,X5 .    @G@@@9.         TITLE - PLUM CODE GENERATOR - REGISTER ALLOCXI
)@@G@@ATOR (LEVEL 3)    @E@@@9. CALL   LINK RGGETXRG             TO OBTAIN X RXJ
)@@G@@EGISTER     @F@@@9. CALL   LINK  RGGETGPR            TO OBTAIN GENERAL RXK
)@@G@@EGISTER     @ @@@9.                           OR@F@@@9.         LINK   RXL
)@@G@@GGETFPR               TO GET FLOATING POINT REG @G@@@9. ACTION  ALLOCATEXM
)@@G@@S ONE REGISTER OF THE TYPE REQUESTED. IF NONE IS FREE @B@@@9.         THXN
)@@G@@E OLDEST ONE IN USE IS STORED @F@@@9. RETURN  X5 POINTS TO REGISTER STATXO
)@@G@@US WORD OF ACQUIRED REGISTER  @#@@@9RGGETXRG   LOCAL .@D@@@9         MOVXP
)@@G@@E  DRGTPE,RGSWXR,I .        SET X REG     @^@@@9         LOAD  A6,0,I . XQ
)@@G@@@D@@@9         GOTO  RGGETMX .           -> COMMON ALLOCATOR@E@@@9RGGETFXR
)@@G@@PR LOCAL .                   GET FLOATING REG 2 WORDS @D@@@9         MOVXS
)@@G@@E  DRGTPE,RGSW2W,I .        SET TO 2 WORDS@C@@@9         GOTO  RGGETM . XT
)@@G@@           -> MERGE     @#@@@9RGGETGPR  LOCAL . @F@@@9         MOVE  DRGXU
)@@G@@TPE,RGSW1W,I .        SET TO 1 WORD CONTENTS    @C@@@9RGGETM   LABEL .  XV
)@@G@@                 MERGE POINT  @C@@@9         LOAD  A6,1,I .            SXW
)@@G@@ET TO A REG @F@@@9RGGETMX  LABEL .                   MERGE X AND A REG AXX
)@@G@@LLOCATOR    @ @@@9         STORE X2,DRGSAV .    @ @@@9         STORE X3,XY
)@@G@@DRGSAV+1 .  @ @@@9         STORE X4,DRGSAV+2 .  @ @@@9         STORE A7,XZ
)@@G@@DRGSAV+3 .  @C@@@9         LOADA A3,RGSWFF .         ASSUME A REG @F@@@9YA
)@@G@@         IF    A6,NE,0,I THEN,RGGETA .     -> CORRECT ASSUMPTION  @C@@@9YB
)@@G@@         LOADA A3,RGSXFF .         X REG PTRS   @#@@@9RGGETA   LABEL .  YC
)@@G@@@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,A3 .    @D@@@9         LOAD  A7,RGSWFL .    YD
)@@G@@     FREE LIST FORWARD  @E@@@9         IF    A7,EQ,A3 THEN,RGNOFREE . ->YE
)@@G@@ FREE LIST EMPTY  @B@@@9         LOAD   X2,RGSWFL .        GET REG@ @@@9YF
)@@G@@         LINK  RGUNLINK .     @C@@@9         LOAD   X3,W1H2+1,A3 .     GYG
)@@G@@ET USED LIST@^@@@9         LINK  RGLINK . @^@@@9         LOAD  X5,X2 .  YH
)@@G@@@C@@@9         GOTO RGEXIT .             -> RETURN    @#@@@9RGNOFREE  LAYI
)@@G@@BEL . @D@@@9         LOAD  X2,W1H1+1,A3 .     GET FIRST USED REG  @G@@@9YJ
)@@G@@          LINK   RGUNLINK .             FREE 1ST REG ON IN USE LIST     YK
)@@G@@@E@@@9         LOAD   X3,W1H2+1,A3 .    ADD TO END OF IN USE LIST @G@@@9YL
)@@G@@          LINK   RGLINK .                 IN-USE LIST (FIFO ORDERING)   YM
)@@G@@@ @@@9         LOAD  X5,X2         .@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5     .YN
)@@G@@@H@@@9         IF    RGSWIU,OFF,RGSWKY THEN,RGX . -> REG NOT IN USE, ALRYO
)@@G@@EADY FREE   @ @@@9         LOAD  X2,RGSWUR     .@G@@@9         LOAD  A3,YP
)@@G@@W1,X2         .  SEE IF ADDRESS WORD POINTS BACK...   @D@@@9         ANDYQ
)@@G@@,U A3,0377777    . GET RID OF KEEP BIT    @E@@@9         IF     A4,NE,X5YR
)@@G@@ THEN,RGX . -> REG ALREADY FREE     @ @@@9         LOADA X3,RGOP1 .     YS
)@@G@@@ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5 .    @ @@@9         LOAD  A4,RGSWKY .    YT
)@@G@@@D@@@9         LOAD  A8,1,I .            SET 1 WORD A REG   @C@@@9      YU
)@@G@@   IF    A4,LT,RGSW2W,I THEN,RGGET2 .     @D@@@9         LOAD  A8,2,I . YV
)@@G@@           SET 2 WORD A REG   @ @@@9         LOADA X3,RGOP2 .     @C@@@9YW
)@@G@@         IF    A4,LT,RGSWXR,I THEN,RGGET2 .     @D@@@9         LOAD  A8,YX
)@@G@@1,I .            SET 1 WORD X REG   @ @@@9         LOADA X3,RGOP3 .     YY
)@@G@@@#@@@9RGGET2   LABEL .  @E@@@9          LINK   XGTMPA .               GEYZ
)@@G@@T TEMP STORAGE    @ @@@9          USING  WORD,X2 .    @^@@@9         STOZA
)@@G@@RE A8,W1H2 .@E@@@9         LOADA A6,AGRX10-AGRX0+AGAW .         NORMAL BZB
)@@G@@ASE   @C@@@9         STORE A6,W1H1 .           SETUP AW     @C@@@9      ZC
)@@G@@   LOADA A6,RGSNULL    . SET UP FAKE AW   @ @@@9         STORE A6,RGSWURZD
)@@G@@     .@E@@@9         STORE A8,CDUFLD .   SET U-FIELD OF INSTRUCTION     ZE
)@@G@@@^@@@9         USING WORD,X3 .@C@@@9         LOAD  A7,W1H2,X3 .         ZF
)@@G@@  GET OP,J  @D@@@9         ADD   A7,RGSWRN .         GET REG NUMBER     ZG
)@@G@@@^@@@9         SLB   A7,4 .   @G@@@9         ADD   A7,10,I .           PZH
)@@G@@UT IN X REGISTER X10 FOR TEMPORARY  @D@@@9         STORE A7,CDINPT,*X10 ZI
)@@G@@.    SET STORE INST     @F@@@9         GCORE 0 .                 ADVANCEZJ
)@@G@@ AND TEST FOR OVERFLOW  @^@@@9         SRB   A7,4 .   @G@@@9         IF ZK
)@@G@@   A7,NE,RGOP3 THEN,RGEXIT . -> X-REG CAN BE ODD OR EVEN    @E@@@9      ZL
)@@G@@   LINK  RGODD .             MAKE SURE A-REG IS ODD   @#@@@9RGX       LAZM
)@@G@@BEL . @#@@@9RGEXIT    LABEL . @ @@@9         USING RGSWRD,X5 .    @C@@@9ZN
)@@G@@         LOAD  A7,DRGTPE .         GET REG TYPE @D@@@9         ADD   A7,ZO
)@@G@@RGSWIU,I .            SET IN USE    @ @@@9         STORE A7,RGSWKY .    ZP
)@@G@@@#@@@9RGXR     LABEL .  @B@@@9         LOAD  A7,DRGSAV+3 .       RETURN ZQ
)@@G@@@ @@@9         LOAD  X4,DRGSAV+2 .  @ @@@9         LOAD  X3,DRGSAV+1 .  ZR
)@@G@@@ @@@9         LOAD  X2,DRGSAV .    @C@@@9         JMP .                ZS
)@@G@@     -> RETURN    @ @@@9RGSNULL   LBLAD  RGSNULL,0    @E@@@9RGOP1    +04ZT
)@@G@@00 .                   SA  OPCODE 01 TO 14 BITS @F@@@9RGOP2    +34640 . ZU
)@@G@@                 DS  OPCODE 71,12 TO 14 BITS    @E@@@9RGOP3    +03000 . ZV
)@@G@@                 SX  OPCODE 06 TO 14 BITS @B@@@9RGOP4    +01576660 .    ZW
)@@G@@     SHIFTED DL   @E@@@9RGMASK   +0377777777777 .    MASK TO 'AND' OUT KZX
)@@G@@EEP BIT     @H@@@9RGMSK2   +0377777000000      . MASK TO EXAMINE H1 POINZY
)@@G@@TERS WITHOUT KEEP BIT   @#@@@9KEPBT1   LABEL .  @C@@@9KEPBIT   SAC   040ZZ
)@@G@@0000,0     . PROTECTED AW FLAG@ @@@9/.       TEMPORARY ALLOCATOR  @D@@@9AA
)@@G@@.        +---------------------+---------------------+@D@@@9.        ! SAB
)@@G@@IZE OF ENTRY       ! BASE ADDRESS        !@D@@@9.        +--------------AC
)@@G@@-------+---------------------+@#@@@9.        ALLOCATOR@D@@@9XGTMPA*  LLOAD
)@@G@@C .                    ALLOCATE TEMPORARY @F@@@9         LOAD  A2,DCGTLVAE
)@@G@@ .         GET CURRENT TEMP STACK LEVEL   @ @@@9         USING TGDSCT,A2AF
)@@G@@ .    @D@@@9         LOAD  A3,TGFSET,A2 .           GET OFFSET    @D@@@9AG
)@@G@@         ADD   A3,TGSIZE,A2 .           GET NEW BASE  @A@@@9         STOAH

)@@G@@OW    @E@@@9         IF    A8,LT,DTGMAX THEN,TGTERM . -> NOPE, RETURN   AK
)@@G@@@E@@@9         STORE A8,DTGMAX .         SET NEW MAX TEMP LEVEL   @#@@@9AL
)@@G@@TGTERM   LABEL .  @^@@@9         USING WORD,X7 .@E@@@9         IF    A2,AM

)@@G@@P .                    -> RETURN    @D@@@9XGTMPF*  LLOC .               AQ

)@@G@@,U A2,0177777 .  REMOVE H AND I BITS@^@@@9         STORE A3,A8 .  @C@@@9AS

)@@G@@@G@@@9         SE,H2 A8,0,*A2 .         SEE IF BASE LESS THAN TEMP ADDR*AW
)@@G@@***** @ @@@9         GOTO  TGWIPE        .@D@@@9         MOVE  TGSIZE+1,AX
)@@G@@-1,I .       SET EMPTY SIZE   @#@@@9TGWIPE   LABEL .  @C@@@9         LOAAY

)@@G@@UTINES@D@@@9.        CODE  GENERATOR ENTRY ROUTINES - GNTR MACRO  @^@@@9BF

)@@G@@FILE) @[@@@V.     @E@@@VCBFILE   LABEL .  STAGGING FOR FILE BIFS RETURNIDE
)@@G@@NG INTEGER  @^@@@V         GNTR    2 .    @D@@@V         LOAD    X2,SGDRDF
)@@G@@SD .        LOAD UP SD OF FILE@G@@@V         STORE   X2,AGX0OF .        DG

)@@G@@      POP OFF FILE STACK ENTRY@E@@@V         MOVE    SGDAID,DCBCLN .    DI

)@@G@@PLA,AGRA3,AGXR0,U .  LOAD FILE SD INTO A3 @ @@@V         GSUB    'BILTN'DK
)@@G@@ .    @ @@@V         GGETGR  AGRL1,1 .    @F@@@V         GINST   OPSA,AGDL
)@@G@@RA3,AGRL1 'NO' . SAVE RESULT FROM BIF     @#@@@VCBNOPXX  GLBL .   @#@@@VDM

)@@G@@.     @A@W@V.                ENDFILE(FILE)  BIF @[@W@V.     @E@W@VCSENDVDO
)@@G@@   LABEL .  STAGING FOR ENDFILE BIF IN VALUE MODE     @^@W@V         GNTDP
)@@G@@R    2 .    @C@W@V         NONPL1 XGFENF,DCBENF,CBFILF .   ENDFILE@#@W@VDQ
)@@G@@CBFILF   LABEL .  @F@W@V         SET 04,ON,DGOPT4 .        SET ENDFILE FDR
)@@G@@UNCTION PRESENT...@C@W@V         LOAD    X2,SGDRSD .        GET FILE SD DS
)@@G@@@B@W@V         XGPOP .  POP OFF FILE STACK ENTRY@D@W@V         MOVE    SDT
)@@G@@GDAID,CBTSTR,2 .  SET STRING TEMP   @E@W@V         STORE   X2,AGX0OF .  DU

)@@G@@ET A TWO WORD TEMP@E@@@W         GINST   OPSA,AGRA2,AGRL2,H1 'NO' . SET MH
)@@G@@INTO FAKE DV@D@@@W         GAPPN   MAXLEN .          FIX TO LOOK LIKE DVMI
)@@G@@@D@W@V         GGETGR  AGXTMP 'X' .       GET AN X REGISTER @D@W@V      MJ
)@@G@@   GINST   OPLA,AGRA1,AGRL1,U .  GET ADDR(DV2)  @D@W@V         GINST   OMK
)@@G@@PLA,AGRA3,AGRL2,U .  GET ADDR(DV1)  @D@W@V         GINST   OPLX,AGXTMP,AML
)@@G@@GRA3 .  STORE PRT-> DV1 @^@W@V         GLIT    2 .    @D@W@V         LA,MM
)@@G@@H1   A2,1,A1 .          GET SIZE OF DV 2  @E@W@V         TG,H1   A2,1,A3MN
)@@G@@ .          IS LEN(STR1)>LEN(STR2)? @E@W@V         GINST   OPLX,AGXTMP,AMO
)@@G@@GRA1 .  NO STORE PRT -> DV2   @F@W@V         GSET    AGRL2+DCGSLT,AGXTMPMP
)@@G@@ .  FIX AW IN BOOL STACK ENTRY@#@W@V         GFIN .   @G@@@W         GFIMQ
)@@G@@N    'POP' .           END OF CODE FOR '&' & '!' OPERATORS  @G@@@W      MR
)@@G@@   GEN .                     FOR BOOL, NEED TO POP OFF EXTRA DEALY@F@@@WMS
)@@G@@         GSET    AGRL2,AGRL1 .     MOVE ADDRESSING DOWN IN STACK  @D@W@VMT
)@@G@@         XGPOP   'SIZE',2*DCGSLT .  POP OF ARGUMENTS  @D@@@W         XGPMU
)@@G@@OP    .                 POP OFF ARGUMENT  @D@W@V         MOVE    SGDAID,MV
)@@G@@CBTSTR,1 .  SET STRING RESULT @D@@@W         MOVE    SGDAID,CBTSTR .    MW
)@@G@@SET STRING RESULT @C@W@V         SET     SGDHLF,ON,SGDID .  SET DV ON   MX
)@@G@@@E@W@V         GOTO    CMSTR2 .           EXIT FROM THIS MESS     @E@@@WMY
)@@G@@         GOTO    GGTRE0 .           EXIT FROM THIS MESS     @^@@@W/.    MZ
)@@G@@   ONCODE BIF     @[@@@W.     @#@@@WCBONCD   LLOC .   @^@@@W         GNTNA
)@@G@@R    2 .    @E@@@W         MOVE    SGDAID,SUMIN .    SAY CONST,FIXED BINNB
)@@G@@(35,0)@E@@@W         LINK    ONUNOK .          SEE IF IN AN ON UNIT     NC

)@@G@@O     @H@@@Z         ADD     A6,ARSTSZ+10+23,I .  FIXED AR +D.V.'S + OFFNG

)@@G@@OFFSET OF ONUNIT MACRO INFO   @E@@@W         MOVE    SGDRAB,AGRX10,I .  NJ

)@@G@@   ROUTINES FOR ONFILE,ONLOC,ONFIELD,ONSOURCE AND ONCHAR    @D@@@XCBONLCOF

)@@G@@     SEE IF WE'RE IN AN ON UNIT     @C@@@X         GOTO    CBONNO .     OS
